                                                                                                                                                                                                  A glimpse
                                                                                                                                                                                                  of reality
                                                                                                                                                                                                 PROPOUND grief and shock
                                                                                                                                                                                                  about what happened to Liver­
                                                                                                                                                                                                  pool fans at Hillsborough is
                                                                                                                                                                                                  n a tu ra l. M any M Ps expressed i t
                                                                                                                                                                                                  yesterday w ith m oving sincerity,
                                                                                                                                                                                                 M r Heffer (Lab, W alton), fo r one, w as
                                                                                                                                                                                                     so overcom e t h a t h e could h a rd ly be
                                                                                                                                                                                                     h eard . H e p u t M s q u estio n to M r
                                                                                                                                                                                                     H u rd {Home S ecretary ) — th e m ost
                                                                                                                                                                                                     difficult question he’d ever p u t in his
                                                                                                                                                                                                     life. Always an emotional man, he
                                                                                                                                                                                                     was plainly afraid of breaking down
                                                                                                                                                                                                     altogether.
                                S M                                                                                                                                                              Many of his constituents were dead and
                                                                                                                                                                                                   injured in a tragedy w hich, as he said,
                                                                                                                                                                                                   o u g ht never to have happened. It m ust
                                                                                                                                                                                                   really, really never happen again.
                                                                                                                                                                                                 He urged M r H u rd to look again, and
                                                                                                                                                                                                   again and again. He m ust look a t
                                                                                                                                                                                                   football fans as civilised h um a n beings,
                                                                                                                                                                                                   not as enem ies of society.
                                                                                                                                                                                                 He m u st ensure th a t they are not
                                                                                                                                                                                                   trapped in football grounds like a n i­
                                                                                                                                                                                                   mals. He m u st ensure th a t ‘th e lovely
                                                                                                                                                                                                   people of Liverpool’ won’t suffer again.
                                                                                                                                                                                                 According to M r D uffy (Lab, Attercliffe),
                                                                                                                                                                                                   th e football au th o rities tre a t th e ir fans
                                                                                                                                                                                                   w ith contem pt. T his they express by
                                                                                                                                                                                                    tutting them in cages, worse treated
                                i   to ld     you     y o u 'd    g o t it w ro n g ! -         i t 's   C h a rlie    C h a p l i n 's c e n t e n a r y '                                         ' an prisoners of w ar in w artim e
                                                                                                                                                                                                   B ritain.
                                                                                                                                                                                                 T he grief of M r David Alton (Democrat,

Post jobs
send
a town
packing
                                                                                 The spice of life . . .
         Daily Mail Reporter
T O W N S F O L K In a
N o rth ern unem ploym ent
blackspot are queueing
up to move South,                                                                                                                                                                                                     iYxvAviv
   More th a n 250 people from
D o n c a s te r h a v e a p p lie d to
become postm en and women in
K ingston upon Tham es, near
London, despite th e higher
living costs.
   Post Office officials in Kings­
ton, w hich has an unem ploy­
m ent rate of only 3 per cent,
recently launched a recru it­
m ent cam paign in th e S outh
Y orkshire town, where th e
jobless total is 14,4 per cent.
 . Homes, flats and bedsits are
being offered by th e Post
Office for workers willing to
m ake th e move. A fter training,
they will earn an average of
£200 a week, plus bonuses.
   ‘We have had a trem endous
response and are still sifting
through th e applications,’ said
Kingston post official Mike
Kevins.
                Response
   ‘We are going to D oncaster
next week to interview 100
applicants and hope to offer all
of them jobs.
   ‘If they come u p to scratch,
we will be back in D oncaster
again and again. We are over­
whelmed by th e response.’
  P ost Office staff a t K ingston
are a t present having to work
overtim e to cope w ith th e
backlog of deliveries.
